(Hankou) The Academic Anti-Japanese General Association held a meeting on the 21st and decided to notify the various schools to organize branch associations, and sent a telegram to Zhang Xueliang, requesting the restoration of lost territories, to be revised and issued later. (21st Dispatch) (Hankou) The Anti-Japanese Association notified the various merchants on the 21st, setting the deadline for registration of enemy goods as the 25th. On the 26th, they will send personnel to check door-to-door. All unregistered goods will be confiscated and the managers will be severely punished. (21st Dispatch)

(Bengbu) The Bengbu Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association Volunteer Army Training Committee was established on the 21st. The committee members are Shangguan Yunxiang, Li Wenbin, Shen Yuanzhen, Xia Yuzhai, and Li Zhuxi. (21st Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Merchants in Xinle County decided to no longer sell Japanese goods. A batch of Japanese goods shipped from Yingkou without a fixed contract has been refused for sale and ordered to be returned to its origin. (21st Dispatch) (Tianjin) The Baoding National Salvation Association organized a volunteer army and hired An Guqin as the chief commander of military training. (21st Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The National Salvation Association of All Circles in Xincheng County stepped up its work, organizing 20 propaganda teams to go to various villages and towns to expand propaganda and arouse the patriotism of the peasants. (21st Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Tianjin United Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association held a standing committee meeting on the 20th and resolved: (1) The work of the merchants' autonomous committee for economic severance of relations with Japan has achieved no results. It should be requested that the city party department order the cessation of work and await investigation. (2) All stations on the Jinpu Railway have absolutely stopped transporting Japanese goods and refuse to load and transport Japanese goods that falsely claim to be domestic brands. (21st Dispatch)

(Yantai) The boycott of Japanese goods here has become increasingly strict. Since last Friday, dock coolies have stopped unloading cargo for Japanese ships. (Reuters dispatch on the 19th)

(Nanjing) Staff members of the Ministry of Industry initiated the study of national martial arts as preparation for self-defense and to jointly meet the national crisis. (21st Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Capital Anti-Japanese Association telegraphed the League of Nations on the 21st, opposing Japan's vested interests in Manchuria and Mongolia. (21st Dispatch) (Hong Kong) The Chinese University has begun forming a volunteer army. (21st Dispatch)

Meeting Held at the Mausoleum

(Nanjing) Chairman Jiang's float was ready tonight, but it was temporarily changed to Madame Kong [Soong Ailing] riding to Shanghai. Jiang did not go tonight, and there was a meeting at the Mausoleum in the evening. (21st Dispatch)

Zhang Xueliang Hopes That Yan and Feng Will Take on Difficult Tasks

Yan Has Expressed Views on the Situation

(Beiping) Nan Guixin sent a telegram to Ping stating that Yan [Xishan] expressed that the entire country should unite against Japan, and there is no better way than internal unity. He himself would not hesitate to sacrifice himself to the utmost. Vice Zhang [Xueliang] hopes that Yan and Feng [Yuxiang] will take on difficult tasks and jointly shoulder the heavy responsibility of national defense. Further measures may be taken after Nan arrives in Ping. It is indeed a fact that Yan telegraphed Zhao Daiwen to return to Jin. Rumors of going to Datong are not true. Feng sent a telegram to Kong Xiangxi expressing his sacrifice of previous personal views and highly praised the Shanghai National Salvation Conference. (21st Dispatch)

Zhang Zuoxiang Arrives in Tianjin

(Tianjin) Zhang Zuoxiang came to Tianjin from Ping on the evening of the 20th and said that this trip was for personal matters and that he would return to Ping in a few days. The Jilin provincial government is controlled by the Japanese, so they plan to move the office to Harbin. Because traffic is blocked, he is temporarily unable to go there. Foreign Important Telegrams

The Situation in Spain is Grave

Parliament urgently passes special legislation

Reuter's 21st, Madrid: Spain may be on the verge of civil war, so Parliament hastily passed a grand plan to defend the republic in a single meeting. One of the provisions authorizes the authorities to severely punish troublemakers, such as those who incite others to riot, incite electrical workers to strike, raise food prices, and unenthusiastic officials. Because unrest is occurring everywhere, the number of unemployed is increasing daily, labor strikes are frequent, and Catholic party members have withdrawn from Parliament, the possibility of civil war is becoming increasingly imminent. It is rumored that members of the Society of Jesus are indignant about the government's anti-religious tendencies and are preparing to resist any government interference or confiscation of their property by force.

Undercurrents Surge in German Political Parties

National, 20th, Berlin: Since Prime Minister Brüning's astonishing victory in the Reichstag last time, huge undercurrents have clearly emerged within the various German political parties. Now there is a danger of them collapsing and overflowing, and this is especially evident between the National People's Party and the Economic Party. The leaders of both parties had issued announcements in advance, ordering their party members in the Reichstag to jointly cast anti-government votes on the vote of no confidence in the cabinet, but the result was the opposite. The entire Economic Party did not approve of the anti-government resolution, and the National People's Party members split into three factions when voting: one was the anti-government faction, one was the pro-government faction, and the other did not express approval or disapproval and did not vote. It is now rumored that the leaders of the Economic Party have proposed punishing the rebel party members, but this proposal was opposed by all party members and could not be established, and they issued a declaration, saying that they were unwilling to bear the heavy responsibility of overthrowing the Brüning cabinet. A portion of the anti-party figures in the National People's Party are mostly directed at the leader Ding Qitai. If there is no definite solution, the anti-party atmosphere may expand further, especially in southern Germany, because southern Germany respects Brüning more than northern Germany.

Austrian Foreign Minister Resolute to Resign

National News Agency, 20th, Vienna: Austrian Foreign Minister Schober has now submitted his resignation to Prime Minister Dr. Boretscher. Boretscher is still considering it. Schober has submitted his resignation twice in the past few weeks. His first resignation was after the failure of the German-Austrian customs union and after returning to Austria after the Geneva meeting. He then withdrew his resignation after being persuaded to stay. The reason for this resignation is that former Prime Minister Seipel vigorously attacked him, making it impossible for him to be at ease in his position. It is said that Schober's resignation this time is quite resolute.

It is rumored that Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov's visit to Turkey this time will put pressure on Turkey to prevent it from joining the League of Nations, which is unfounded. This point was stated earlier when Turkish Foreign Minister Rüştü met with French Foreign Minister Briand. Kemal also stated regarding the upcoming Second Balkan Conference that the only slogan for this meeting is the four words "peace and friendship," which are also Turkey's diplomatic policy. In addition to the full attendance of the Balkan Peninsula countries at the Second Balkan Conference, other European countries such as Germany, France, and Italy will have informal representatives participating as observers.

National, 20th, Paris: The American Federal Reserve Bank has recently established an agreement with the French Banque de France. The agreement has been signed in New York by the presidents of the two banks. The agreement states that regarding the withdrawal of cash from the Banque de France in the United States, the Banque de France declares that it is willing to deposit 200 million gold dollars as the minimum amount to be retained in the United States, and the American side declares that it will do its best to guarantee the safety of the gold standard and will give a slightly higher deposit interest rate.

Important News

The League of Nations Ends the Manchurian Incident Haphazardly

The Executive Yuan's Standing Committee closed on the 30th

The demands made by our representative have not been resolved

Geneva Special Dispatch: Regarding the Manchurian Incident, it has been almost two weeks since our representative handed it over to the League of Nations Executive Council for resolution. Our country has not made the slightest progress so far. The several demands made by our representative Shi Zhaoji have not received satisfactory replies, such as (1) requesting Japan to withdraw its troops as soon as possible and restore the pre-war state, (2) requesting Japan to compensate for the losses suffered due to its aggression, (3) requesting the League of Nations to organize an investigative committee to observe the truth of the incident, and (4) advocating that the Executive Council be responsible for resolving the matter and opposing Japan's proposal for direct negotiations. Regarding items (2), (3), and (4), because the Japanese representative insisted on opposing them, our side did not make fierce rebuttals, so the above three items have so far yielded no results, and the Executive Council has also turned a deaf ear. Regarding the withdrawal of troops as soon as possible, the chairman of the Executive Council once advised the Chinese and Japanese troops to withdraw to their respective national defense areas. This method is not only ridiculous, but also illogical. This time, Japan is attacking us alone, and the Chinese troops are in a position of being attacked and have not left Chinese territory by a single step. Now the Executive Council orders the Chinese troops to withdraw at the same time as the Japanese troops. Where should the Chinese troops withdraw to? This is already unreasonable, and what is more, the Japanese troops have not only not withdrawn so far, but are increasing daily. The Japanese representative said that the Japanese troops have withdrawn a portion, which is simply a cover-up. Although the Executive Council knows that it is a lie by the Japanese representative, it has to pretend to be deaf and dumb for fear of Japan's arrogance. This kind of ostrich-like method is completely contrary to the purpose of the League of Nations to maintain peace. No wonder the actions of the Council this time have been strongly criticized by impartial people all over the world.

On the afternoon of September 30th, the League of Nations Executive Council held a closing meeting. First, the chairman read aloud to the meeting the results of the "Five-Headed Conference." The so-called "Five-Headed Conference" was a preliminary meeting of representatives from England, France, Italy, Germany, and Spain. The major plans of the Executive Council are decided here. Its nature is equivalent to the "Three-Headed Conference" of the Paris Peace Conference era, so the Executive Council meeting is only a formality on the surface. The results of this "Five-Headed Conference" are translated as follows:

1. The Executive Council has learned that the governments of China and Japan have replied to the urgent advice given by the chairman of the Council and has learned that the two governments have taken various measures in accordance with this advice.

2. The Council considers the Japanese government's statement that it has no intention of occupying Manchuria to be very important. (Note: Japan has been planning to annex Manchuria for a long time.)

3. The Council is aware of the statement made by the Japanese government that the government will, within the scope possible, quickly withdraw its troops that have already begun to return to the railway boundary.

Page 9

Continuation of Important News

limit, but the safety of the lives and property of the Japanese people must have a definite guarantee, and the Japanese government hopes that this wish will be realized soon.

4. The Council has learned of the Chinese representative's statement that the government will, after the Japanese troops withdraw one after another and the Chinese police and local authorities are restored, assume full responsibility for the safety of the lives and property of the Japanese people living outside the railway boundary. (Note: Our authorities have never shirked their responsibility to protect Japanese nationals.)

5. The Council has learned that the Chinese and Japanese representatives have guaranteed that their respective governments will take necessary measures to prevent the incident from escalating. Therefore, the Council firmly believes that the two governments have the desire to maintain peace and friendly relations between the two countries.

6. The Council requests both parties to restore past friendly relations as soon as possible and hopes that the two governments should immediately fulfill the above-mentioned obligations that have already been promised.

7. The Council requests both parties to make complete reports to the Council on the progress of this matter in the future.

8. The Council decided to convene another special meeting on October 14th (Wednesday) to discuss the situation regarding this matter at that time, but if any unexpected emergency occurs, the Council can convene earlier.

9. The Chairman of the Executive Council, regarding the progress of this incident,

Upon consulting with the members, the representatives of China and Japan, or others, if it is considered that there is no need to convene a meeting on October 14th, the chairman may cancel the decision to convene the meeting.

After the chairman of the Executive Council read it aloud, the Japanese representative immediately spoke to express his approval. The representative of our country stated that he reserved our country's claim for compensation for losses and said that he hoped that the Japanese troops should be completely withdrawn before October 14th, otherwise China would take necessary measures, etc. Finally, the chairman said that if there were no other opinions at the meeting, it would be considered unanimously approved. The meeting adjourned after he spoke. Looking at the results of this meeting comprehensively, Japan has won completely. What our country has obtained from the League of Nations is only a piece of paper with black and white writing. I wonder what the readers will think when they see this.

The failure of our country's diplomacy this time and the suspicion that the League of Nations Executive Council is partial to Japan are undeniable facts, and the weakness of our country's diplomatic personnel in negotiations is also undeniable. This time, our country requested the Executive Council to resolve the Manchurian Incident based on the provisions of Article 11 of the League of Nations Covenant. According to this article, any member state has the right to draw the League of Nations' attention when two countries are at war. The so-called "any member state" refers to a third country other than those at war, and its purpose is to maintain peace and does not involve matters such as compensation or organizing an investigative committee. For the convenience of readers, the original text of Article 11 is translated as follows: "(1) ... Any war or threat of war, whether it directly affects member states of this League or not, is a matter of concern to the entire League of Nations, and the League of Nations shall immediately adopt appropriate methods to ensure international peace. Under these circumstances, the Secretary-General shall immediately convene the Executive Council at the request of any member state. (2) ... In the event of a situation affecting international relations and sufficient to disturb world peace or harm the friendly relations on which peace depends, any member state, in the name of friendship, has the right to draw the attention of the League of Nations Assembly or the Executive Council." After reading it, we will know that the establishment of this article is aimed at third countries other than those in dispute. Now our country is clearly a country involved and not a third country. What is requested from the Executive Council is to sanction Japan's military aggression and demand compensation for the losses suffered due to the aggression. Now our country is requesting the Executive Council based on Article 11, which can truly be said to be irrelevant. According to the provisions of Article 11, the responsibility of the Executive Council is only to maintain international peace and does not have the power to resolve "punishing the culprit" and "compensation." Our country spent two weeks and did not get the slightest result, which is also due to this reason.

Japan's actions this time clearly violated the provisions of Articles 12, 13, and 15 of the League of Nations Covenant. These three articles state that if member states have disputes, they should resolve them by peaceful means and should never resort to war. Those who violate them should be punished according to Article 16 of the same Covenant. The original text of Article 16 is translated as follows: "(1) If a member state resorts to war in disregard of its covenants under Articles 12, 13, or 15, it shall ipso facto be deemed to have committed an act of war against all other members of the League, which hereby undertake immediately to subject it to the severance of all trade or financial relations, the prohibition of all intercourse between their nationals and the nationals of the covenant-breaking State, and the prevention of all financial, commercial or personal intercourse between the nationals of the covenant-breaking State and the nationals of any other State, whether a Member of the League or not. (2) It shall be the duty of the Council in such case to recommend to the several governments concerned what effective military, naval or air force the Members of the League shall severally contribute to the armed forces to be used to protect the covenants of the League. (3) ... The members of the League agree, further, that they will mutually support one another in the financial and economic measures which are taken under this Article, in order to minimize the loss and inconvenience resulting from the above measures, and that they will mutually support one another in resisting any special measures aimed at one of their number by the covenant-breaking State. ... (4) Any Member of the League which has violated any covenant of the League may be declared to be no longer a Member of the League." Japan, using the pretext that China cannot protect its nationals and that the Chinese army destroyed the South Manchuria Railway, directly sent troops to Manchuria, which is clearly an act that violates the League of Nations Covenant, so Article 16 should be applied to punish it. If our country needs to request compensation for losses or organize an investigative committee, then Article 15 should be applied. However, our country's representative did not consider this and requested the League of Nations Executive Council to resolve the matter based on Article 11. What is their intention? We cannot measure their profoundness. (October 1)

Outbreak of War in Longjiang

Zhang Haipeng Leads Troops to Invade Heilongjiang Province

Yu Zhaolin Tenaciously Defends Jiangqiao Station and Inflicts Heavy Blows

Ma Zhanshan Appointed Acting Chairman of Heilongjiang Province

The Reasons Behind the Recent Incident

Harbin Dispatch: Zhang Haipeng, the garrison commander of Taonan, incited by the Japanese army, led his troops northward on the 14th to invade Heilongjiang. The Heilongjiang Provincial Government Committee, having received a telegram from the Deputy Commander's Office in Beiping, denounced Zhang's reliance on Japanese power as a rebellious act. Considering the temporary involvement of Japanese influence, the committee decided to tolerate the situation for the time being. To ensure the safety of the provincial capital, they chose a peaceful retreat and relocated the troops to a secure location, postponing further discussion until the Northeast China-Japan issue was resolved. Consequently, Provincial Committee members Zhao Zhongren, Dou Lianfang, and others left the province for Harbin on the evening of the 14th. Wan Fulin's family members also sought refuge in Harbin. Only a small number of police officers remained in the provincial capital to maintain order. Fearing looting by Zhang's troops during the transition in the provincial capital, merchants in the capital dispatched representatives to Tailai Town on the evening of the 14th to welcome Zhang's army. Zhang's army had planned to occupy Longsha on the morning of the 15th. At 6 PM on the 14th, a brigade of cavalry and over 7,000 Mongolian soldiers colluded with them and arrived at Tailai Town on three trains. At 8 PM, they continued their advance, reaching the area of Kaerge. Suddenly, Yu Zhaolin's brigade at Jiangqiao Station blew up the bridge, halting Zhang's army's progress. Many of the soldiers in this brigade were former members of Han Guangdi's brigade during the anti-Russian campaign in the 18th year of the Republic (1929). Enraged by Zhang's arrogance, they disobeyed their brigade commander's orders and, with all 5,000 men, defended the area, preventing Zhang's army from advancing. Unable to cross, Zhang's army stopped there. On the morning of the 16th, Yu's brigade launched a fierce cross-river attack on Zhang's army at dawn, with intense artillery fire, inflicting significant losses on Zhang's army, which retreated several miles. At noon, two Japanese aircraft provided cover for the cavalry of Zhang's brigade as they attacked Yu's brigade. The aircraft dropped several heavy bombs. Despite their smaller numbers, Yu's troops were highly motivated and resisted desperately. The fierce battle continued until dusk and resumed in the evening, and there has been no definite news up to this morning. However, Gao Renfu, the director of the Xing'an Reclamation Bureau, has led the Sun and Wang regiments from the Solun Mountain area to attack the rear of Zhang's army, assisting Yu's brigade in a pincer movement. Zhang's army is now facing enemies on both sides and cannot succeed. At the same time, Wu Songshan's 1st Cavalry Brigade from Zhaodong and Zhang Zhanjiu's 2nd Cavalry Brigade from Fularji are rushing to Jiangqiao Station to assist Yu's brigade. Zhang's troops are mostly cavalry, lack heavy artillery, and have little actual combat experience, making them inferior to Yu's brigade and the reclamation troops. The situation is expected to be resolved within a day or two. Zhang Jinghui, the chief of the Special District administration, is an old friend of Zhang Haipeng. Seeing Zhang in dire straits, he sent his advisor, Lei Chun, to Jiangqiao on the evening of the 14th to persuade both sides to cease hostilities and for Zhang's troops to return to Taonan. The distant cause of Zhang's armed rebellion is that Zhang and the late Zhang Zuolin and Wu Junsheng were very close friends. He is considered a veteran among the warlords in the Northeast. His cavalry is brave and skilled in battle. After Wu Junsheng was promoted to the position of Military Governor of Heilongjiang in the 13th year of the Republic (1924), Zhang succeeded Wu as the garrison commander of Taoliao and has held the position for many years, gaining considerable prestige in the Mongolian border area. After Wu Junsheng's death, when the position of Military Governor of Heilongjiang became vacant, Zhang felt that he was the most qualified candidate. However, the position was taken by Wan Fulin, which made him quite unhappy. Later, when Zhang Xueliang took office and appointed Zou Zuohua as the Director of the Xing'an Reclamation Bureau, Zhang's influence was greatly reduced, and Xueliang did not treat Zhang (Haipeng) very well. As a result, Zhang became increasingly depressed. Recently, with the Japanese occupation of Liaoning and Jilin, they incited Zhang. After Prince Gong arrived in Liaoning, he named Zhang as the General of Heilongjiang in the name of the Ming Dynasty Empire. Zhang was still hesitant and had not yet made a decision. His son, Zhiming, was fascinated by the power of the Crown Prince and urged his father, also contacting the Japanese consulate in Tongliao. On the 5th of this month, 10,000 rifles and 400,000 rounds of ammunition were delivered, and Zhang finally made up his mind. He then colluded with Mongolian bandits, detained the Tao'ang train, and Zhang Zhiming went to Heilongjiang on the 9th to directly demand political power from the Heilongjiang provincial government. Zhang is now 67 years old and nearing the end of his life. His old friends are very saddened by this act of treason. Before Zhang launched his rebellion, Wan Fulin, seeing that no one was in charge of provincial affairs and that he could not immediately return north, discussed the matter with Deputy Commander Zhang and agreed to resign from the position of chairman and appoint Ma Zhanshan, the garrison commander of Heihe, as acting chairman. Ma led his troops to Longsha on the morning of the 16th and took office at noon, suppressing unrest. With someone in charge of the Heilongjiang provincial government, Zhang Haipeng's rebellion is not a cause for concern. Here is Wan Fulin's telegram to the elders of Heilongjiang Province from Beiping: "Fulin was ordered to enter the customs due to military affairs and has been away for five months. I am extremely disturbed by the long absence from my duties. Just as I thought the military affairs were over and I could return to the province, the Shenyang Incident of September 18th occurred. Jiang Province is located on the border, with vast territory and few soldiers. Foreign aggression is worrying, and the uprisings of bandits and Red elements are concerning. The occurrence of incidents is unpredictable. Fulin is stranded in Beiping and cannot return immediately, making it difficult to manage affairs remotely. I have now submitted a request to Deputy Commander Zhang and asked the National Government to remove me from the position of chairman of the provincial government and appoint a capable person to take charge. I only remember that Fulin has been governing Jiang for three years and has been gradually developing industries and schools to help the people's livelihood and enlighten knowledge. Now, I have stopped halfway and have nothing to show for it, which is deeply regrettable. But at this time of hardship, people's hearts are fluctuating, and conspiracies and heresies are easily agitated. A little carelessness can lead to the destruction of security, and the consequences are unimaginable. I hope that my elders and children will warn each other not to be moved by rumors or misled by fallacies. Everyone should settle down in their own business so as not to do evil. Internal security is the prerequisite for resisting foreign aggression. These are the words that Fulin cannot help but say. I hope you all will take them to heart." (16th)

Taonan Dispatch: After being incited by the Japanese, Zhang Haipeng, the garrison commander of Taoliao, carried out a rebellion and sent troops to invade Heilongjiang. The details of the situation are recorded as follows. Zhang Haipeng originally came from the banditry, known as "Daxiang." After surrendering, his army was quite despised by the general public because his army had no order. Zhang was ridiculed because of his dark face full of pockmarks, therefore another nickname called "Zhang Da Mazi." Zhang's personality is very simple. After the Liaoning-Jilin Incident, he immediately convened a meeting of the Taonan county magistrate and local gentry and merchants. Zhang was the first to speak, saying that since the provincial capital had fallen, if the Japanese army advanced to this place (i.e., Taonan), we should express our welcome to avoid the people suffering from the ravages of war. At that time, all the participants in the meeting agreed with Zhang's proposal and unanimously approved it. Later, on the 25th of last month, a small number of Japanese troops arrived in Taonan and immediately stayed at Zhang's private residence. In addition to guiding the Japanese soldiers to visit various places every day, Zhang also secretly discussed the plan for independence with the Japanese day and night. One day, Zhang led the Japanese to visit the Taonan Private Zhuqing School, which was founded by Wu's wife, Ms. Li Zhuqing, with private funds of hundreds of thousands of yuan, and was quite large in scale. When visiting the auditorium, Zhang saw the portrait of Sun Yat-sen hanging on the wall and immediately criticized it to please the Japanese. The school feared Zhang's power and had to remove Sun Yat-sen's portrait. By the end of last month, his rebellion plan had matured. Zhang led his troops to harass Heilongjiang. The Japanese promised to supply Zhang's troops with 20,000 large rifles, and ammunition would be replenished at any time. Up to now, the Japanese have transported a total of six trains of machinery and ammunition to Taonan, including more than 6,000 rifles and more than 2 million rounds of ammunition, all of which were produced by the Northeast Arsenal. The first batch arrived at Taonan Station on the first of this month. On the evening of the 3rd, the ammunition truck suddenly retreated one station from Taonan. Zhang had dispatched more than a dozen cars in advance to wait there. When the ammunition truck arrived, all the ammunition was unloaded and transported to the garrison commander's office by Zhang's cars. The train immediately rushed back to Shenyang. The next day, Zhang claimed that the Japanese ammunition was intended to supply Mongolian bandits and had been rejected by him and returned to Shenyang. Zhang was very happy to receive this large batch of machinery and ammunition, so he convened his subordinates to hold secret meetings day and night to discuss the conspiracy to attack Heilongjiang. Zhang's subordinates unanimously elected Zhang as the Commander-in-Chief of Border Defense. At the same time, eight major offices were organized, and directors of each office were assigned. The matter was heard by the subordinates of the new favorites, such as orderlies, and they were all happily showing joy, so they spread the word everywhere. Later, it was heard by the station master of Taonan Station on the Taoang Railway, and the station master immediately telegraphed Wan Guobin, the director of the Taoang Railway Bureau, to report that Zhang Haipeng had a secret plan to attack Heilongjiang. After receiving the telegram, Wan not only transferred all the vehicles on the entire line to Ang'angxi, but also telegraphed Zhang Haipeng to test his intentions. The general idea of ​​the telegram was: "The Heilongjiang province area is important, and my father is in Ping. Colleagues unanimously welcome you (referring to Mr. Zhang) to Heilongjiang to help preside over everything." After receiving the telegram, Zhang thought that the Heilongjiang province had welcomed him to come, as desired, so he replied that he had been repeatedly oppressed by the Japanese in Tao and was planning to go to Heilongjiang to take refuge temporarily. After reading this telegram, Wan knew that Zhang was indeed intending to attack Heilongjiang, so he sent Zhang another urgent telegram, saying that he had just received an urgent telegram from the Deputy Commander, saying that Taonan was the first gateway to Heilongjiang and was of great importance to Heilongjiang province, so please do not give it up lightly. After reading this telegram, Zhang thought that since Wan had telegraphed to stop him, he figured that the opportunity had been leaked, so he decided to launch immediately. At that time, Taonan was repairing barracks, and there were more than a thousand workers. Zhang ordered that all the workers be changed into soldiers and organized into regiments, with the head foreman as the regimental commander, and the other small foremen as battalion commanders, company commanders, platoon leaders, etc. At the same time, the machinery, ammunition, and clothing supplied by the Japanese and transported from the Northeast Clothing Factory were all distributed to the workers for use. They then marched to Heilongjiang. However, most of these workers had property in the local area, so many of them fled back midway. Zhang then recruited Mongolian bandits and moved towards Wu Tai Bei. On the way, they first encountered the reclamation army and immediately bombarded each other. The Mongolian bandits were mostly scattered, but the reclamation army was afraid of being outnumbered, so they retreated and joined forces with the Heilongjiang army. They are now prepared to defeat the rebel army. (October 17)

Japanese Release of Sino-Japanese Notes on Troop Withdrawal Issue

The National Government had sent a note to the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting that in accordance with the resolution of the League of Nations, Japanese troops occupying the territory be withdrawn by October 14, and that China take over and be responsible for restoring security in various places. Japan replied to the note, refusing to comply. The National Government then sent another note, continuing the previous proposal, but the Japanese side did not respond. The aforementioned notes are of great importance. When Ambassador Jiang sent the first note, because it contained a deadline for troop withdrawal, the international press temporarily regarded it as containing the nature of an ultimatum, and there was much speculation and whispering. However, the original text has not yet been released by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. According to the Osaka Asahi Shimbun, the aforementioned notes have been released by the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and we are translating them as follows:

Ambassador Jiang's Note to Shidehara: "I received a telegram from our Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the 4th of this month stating that the representative of the Japanese government formally declared in the League of Nations that the Japanese troops currently occupying various places should be withdrawn as soon as possible, and that the state before September 18 should be restored. The final resolution of the Executive Yuan also stated that the Japanese troops should be withdrawn entirely before the meeting on the 14th of this month. The National Government has already telegraphed Deputy Commander Zhang on the 2nd of this month to appoint the commander of the troops in various places so that they can take over various places after the withdrawal of the Japanese troops and be responsible for restoring security in various places. The deputy commander has now selected Zhang Zuoxiang and Wang Shuchang to take over. I pray that you will notify the Japanese government to order the Japanese troops to contact the takeover officers sent by our side to complete the handover before the 14th of this month." October 5,

Shidehara's Reply to Ambassador Jiang's Note: "Regarding the troop withdrawal mentioned in your note, the Japanese representative in the League of Nations stated that the premise for Japan's... to the attached territories is that the safety of railways and the lives and property of Japanese subjects in Manchuria can be ensured. As for the resolution of the Administrative Council of the League of Nations on September 30, there is no provision that the Japanese troops should be withdrawn entirely before the reopening of the meeting on the 14th. Regarding the matters mentioned in the second half of your note, the Japanese government's views are as follows: 1. Since the conflict between the Japanese and Chinese troops near Fengtian in the middle of the night on September 18, the Japanese troops have begun to operate on the entire line in Manchuria. This is because there were superior troops stationed around them, and they had to strike first to eliminate the threat. Although the Chinese troops declared a policy of non-resistance at that time, they actually tried to resist everywhere, causing many casualties to the Japanese troops. 2. Although the Chinese government has declared that it will send Zhang Zuoxiang and Wang Shuchang to contact the Japanese troops to take over the task of maintaining security in various places after the withdrawal of the Japanese troops, if the Chinese troops are armed and assembled in various places, even if their purpose is to maintain local security, the Japanese troops cannot help but feel the same major threat as at the time of the outbreak of the incident. Moreover, when the feelings of the people of China and Japan are excited, the danger of conflict between the troops of the two countries is even greater. 3. The Japanese government believes that the urgent task at present is to ease the feelings of the people. Therefore, the two countries should quickly agree on several basic outlines that can serve as the foundation for establishing normal relations. After the agreement on these outlines, when the feelings of the people are eased, the Japanese troops can withdraw entirely into the South Manchuria Railway attached territory. At the same time, the task of taking over security maintenance can also be easily and satisfactorily implemented. 4. The Japanese government can at any time consult with the responsible Chinese representatives on the aforementioned fundamental outlines." October 9,

Glimpses of Jilin

British and American Embassy Staff Come to Jilin for Inspection

Xi Qia Hires Three More Japanese Advisors

Mr. Hipple Myers, the U.S. Consul General in Shenyang, Mr. George Hanson, the U.S. Consul General in Harbin, and Mr. Sussabury, the second secretary of the U.S. Embassy in Japan, came to Jilin a few days ago to inspect everything and meet with Chinese and Japanese authorities. They have now completed their work and left Jilin. In addition, two counselors from the British Embassy in China, along with the British Consul General in Liaoning, a group of three people, came to Jilin today (the 15th) to investigate everything. The Japanese army searched various schools above the middle school level, confiscating many books, most of which were related to the Three People's Principles and Japan, and declared that they would be severely punished if they were found again.

The Japanese military authorities believe that the news about the Eastern Provinces published in the Chinese newspapers in China proper is not conducive to them. They notified the postal authorities the day before yesterday that they were not allowed to deliver them. Therefore, newspapers such as Shen Xin and Dagong have disappeared in Jilin and only the Chinese-Japanese newspapers such as Taidong and Manchuria Shengjing are seen.

General Shigeru Honjo, commander of the Japanese Kwantung Army, arrived in Jilin today on the Jilin-Changchun train. Xi Qia personally welcomed him. After Honjo inspected the Japanese army, he returned to Shenyang on the afternoon of 5 o'clock.

Xi Qia, at the request of the Japanese army, hired Lieutenant Colonel Omote Michiki, the former Japanese military advisor to the Border Defense, as the military advisor to the pseudo-chief executive's office, and also hired Yūichi Hamada, director of the Mantetsu Public Office, and Masaaki Mitsuhashi, chairman of the Resident Association, as political advisors.

The Provincial Post Office has suspended the opening of money orders to postal areas outside of Jilin and Heilongjiang since yesterday (the 14th), and the money houses have also stopped remittances, thus cutting off the economic ties between China proper and abroad.

Xi Qia appointed Jin Bidong (Prince Su of the Qing Dynasty) as the director of the Jilin-Changchun and Jilin-Dundhua Railway Bureaus and the head of the Changchun Municipal Preparation Office. Jin holds three important positions concurrently, all due to the power of the Japanese. It is said that Jin's sisters are all married to Japanese, and his wife is also Japanese, making him completely Japanized.

Hiberly, a British reporter for the Shenyang International News Agency, and a group of five people arrived in Jilin a few days ago to investigate the truth about Jilin. (October 15)

Li Youlan Talks About the Situation in Shenyang

Tianjin News: Li Youlan, the supervisor of the Benxi Lake Coal Mine Company, was a member of the local maintenance association initiated after the Liaoning Incident last month. He arrived in Tianjin from Shenyang the day before yesterday. A reporter made a special visit to interview him. Mr. Li talked about the details of the Shenyang Local Maintenance Association in great detail, saying, "After the incident on the night of the 18th of last month, I (Li, I referred to myself) immediately sent someone to risk finding the Chinese manager of Okura Gumi on the next morning, informed the director of Okura Gumi and conveyed my intention: the area must not be allowed to deteriorate, and they should find a way to maintain it. The director of Okura Gumi agreed with this and immediately visited the Japanese Consul General. The Consul also agreed, but said that he would have to wait for Commander Honjo to arrive before discussing it. On the afternoon of the 19th, Honjo arrived and also agreed. However, he said that he should notify his military police captain, and that he could do his best to accommodate our gentry and merchants' opinions on matters of security in the city. We then tried to find the military police captain, and finally met him in the evening. I raised two points: first, please maintain the electric light factory; second, please maintain the telephone. We will talk about the rest tomorrow. The Japanese followed suit. However, according to the Japanese military's opinion, it was not until a week later that the establishment of a maintenance association was allowed, so it was delayed for several days before it was established. When I first proposed it, Chairman Zang had already agreed, but then Chairman Zang and Jin, the director of education, were both under surveillance, and the people had no leader. I then requested Mr. Yuan Jinkai to take responsibility for maintaining it. Mr. Zhao Xinbo was also invited by us. After the maintenance association was established, there was Jin Liang, who was proposed by the Japanese. We had no objections. We have repeatedly stated to the Japanese that the maintenance association is only responsible for local security, finance, and commerce, and does not concern itself with political issues. After its establishment, it has been working according to this policy. The security police have increased from 600 to 2,000 people, and shops have gradually opened. The Bank of Communications and the Bank of China have resumed business. However, the Japanese initially refused to allow the official bank of the Three Eastern Provinces and the Border Industry Bank to resume business, which took a lot of talking. Later, on the 10th of this month, that is, National Day, at a meeting at the South Manchuria Railway Station, the Japanese proposed that Japanese advisors and inspectors be set up in each department of the official bank. We told them that it was enough to send one person to temporarily check the accounts to understand the contents at any time, so why send so many advisors? But the Japanese insisted on their proposal, and the proposals we made were not passed. At this time, I felt that Shenyang could no longer be stayed. I have not been in politics for years, but have been managing official business. This incident has caused panic and danger among the people to the extreme. In order to reduce the suffering of the people, I cannot but come out and use the status of the people to temporarily mediate, but I am confident that my colleagues' patriotism is no less than that of others, and I will never do anything to harm the country. Although the general public does not understand and gives me a bad name, the facts will eventually be revealed, so I have no guilt in my heart. I often said in Shenyang, if there is anything that harms the country, I should be shot, not just scolded. That is my one-month-old opinion. However, at the meeting on the 10th, the Japanese ordered us to add a word to the official bank number. I thought that if this continues, we will gradually fall into a vortex and lose my original intention of maintaining the place. Therefore, I did not go home that night after the meeting and left Shenyang the next morning. I have no other intention in coming to Tianjin. I will report to Deputy Commander Zhang in Ping once and then return to Tianjin to be a temporary citizen of Tianjin. As for Benxi Lake, because the Japanese have expelled the Chinese cadres, I have no way to serve there."

Page 10

The reporter then asked how the Japanese were spreading the movement for an independent government. Mr. Li replied, "It hasn't reached the point of compulsion. No official Japanese person in charge has approached us, but there are very many Japanese who are spreading and persuading this matter. They are all related to the Japanese military. We have repeatedly and earnestly told these people that this matter is impossible, not only because we have no political ambitions but also because we have a patriotic ideology and cannot do it, and it will be ineffective because there is no basis. The Chinese government will definitely attack us in the future, so we must rely on Japanese protection to be safe. May I ask, what will international opinion think of Japan at that time? Therefore, even for the sake of Japan, since you say you are not occupying the land, you should not cause such trouble. We also said that if you want to form a government, you must ask Chairman Zang to come out. The people still only recognize Zang as the chairman. The chairman also said so. I immediately said that since you agree, can we all start publicizing this matter from today? The Japanese man said that this needs to be considered separately, because many knowledgeable Japanese expatriates do not agree with the military's extreme actions, but they absolutely dare not say so. People from the consulate also said that during this military period, it is inconvenient for consulate personnel to advocate anything, so the rest can be known. The director of Okura Gumi, who has been working hard for the maintenance association, has been blamed by military figures, who said he was biased towards China. The arrogance of the military can be known. Because the Japanese were ineffective in finding us, they turned to find others. I heard that Zhang Xian is one of those they are looking for, but I don't know the details. As for the Shenyang area, it is not easy for them to find people, because the Japanese must choose someone who is well-known in society. Since we are not doing it and Yan Zhaoxi is not doing it, Yan has disbanded his Four People's Association and is the vice-chairman of the local maintenance association. After I left Shenyang, I heard that the Japanese were very unhappy. Later, Mr. Yuan Jinkai signed on my behalf. Mr. Yuan's aim is not to talk about forming a government, not to talk about independence, but to maintain it for one day if he can. If he is forced to be independent, he will also withdraw from the maintenance association and no longer care about anything."

Shantou Citizens United in Anti-Japanese Resistance

Shantou Correspondence: Japanese soldiers have occupied the two provinces of Liaoning and Jilin, not only showing no sincerity in withdrawing their troops but instead protesting to the government and demanding the use of force to suppress the patriotic movement of the masses. On the 12th, the Japanese consul stationed in Shantou presented four demands to the Shantou Municipal Government: (1) tear down anti-Japanese slogans on all streets; (2) dispatch police to protect Chinese workers; (3) order Chinese merchants to sell food to the Japanese; and (4) allow Japanese sailors to land to protect Japanese residents. The Municipal Government found these four demands difficult to fulfill and intolerable. The Japanese warship "Tayo" has been in Shantou for many days, with Sakasaka & Co. acting as its food supplier. The warship dispatches a small motorboat to transport supplies from the city. The Municipal Party Headquarters, recognizing the severity of the national crisis, decided on the 13th to send a letter to the Shantou Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, immediately convening all sectors to hold an anti-Japanese demonstration parade. Furthermore, on the 12th, the Shantou Labor Circle National Salvation Association held a joint meeting, electing representatives from the sewing, shipping, stevedoring, railway transport, civilian shipping, United Safety, telegraph, postal, Shantou camphor nine associations as the presidium. It was decided that at 9:00 AM on the 18th, all labor unions would gather at Zhongshan Road to hold a worker demonstration parade. Each team would be responsible for its own order and discipline. Zhang Lingyun and Xu Pingqing initiated the Lingdong People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Volunteer Army, and many men and women have been enthusiastically signing up in recent days. On the 12th, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce held an inaugural preparatory meeting, electing Zhang Lingyun and 16 others as preparatory committee members. The office is temporarily located in Zhongshan Park. The Anti-Japanese National Congress first allocated 200 yuan as temporary preparatory expenses. Xiao Yunge and three others were appointed to draft recruitment regulations for the volunteer corps and training rules, with training to begin on November 1st. Additionally, students from secondary schools and above in Shantou have been responsible for investigating and sealing off Japanese goods in designated areas of the city since the 6th. This work is nearly halfway complete, and merchant groups have requested the Anti-Japanese Association to continue the sealing. The Student Anti-Japanese Federation issued a notice today that from the 14th to the 19th, all secondary school students and above will suspend classes to investigate and seal off enemy goods. They also posted notices to all merchants, requiring them to fill out forms listing the names of the goods and apply for sealing within five days, sending people to shout announcements with gongs. Any goods that are missed and not sealed will be sealed within these five days. After this period, if any more enemy goods are discovered, they will be treated as smuggling enemy goods and punished accordingly. Jiao Guang Middle School and Yu Huai Middle School are expanding their anti-Japanese propaganda, dividing into teams to go to nearby cities, towns, and villages to give national salvation speeches. Since the 13th, students have been standing on major thoroughfares, recounting the painful history of national subjugation. Also, on the 12th, Christians and students from church-run schools and kindergartens throughout the city gathered on Zhongshan Road for a parade, marking a new record of Christian participation in the national salvation movement. On that day, Lin Tianduo, Fu Shang, and Chen Zelin were publicly elected as the presidium to hold religious ceremonies, pray for national peace, and sing hymns of Christian soldiers. Resolutions were passed: (1) to telegraph Christians across the country to unite and save China from its peril; (2) to telegraph a request to cease internal strife and jointly resist foreign aggression; (3) to telegraph Japanese Christians, requesting them to uphold justice and maintain peace; (4) to telegraph Christian churches worldwide, advocating justice and maintaining world peace. The Christian parade was extremely orderly, with no slogans advocating overthrow or declaring war. Shantou newspapers have been publishing national salvation and anti-Japanese news from various counties, occupying nearly nine-tenths of the entire space. Telegrams from various groups advocate a united declaration of war against Japan, but in reality, there is little preparation and no concrete plan. On the other hand, the Japanese in Shantou are fully prepared for everything. Women and children have already returned to their country last week. Japanese elementary schools and Toyo schools have been closed. Each time a Japanese ship goes to Taiwan or Shanghai, Japanese naval personnel change into plain clothes and help their expatriates move luggage and important bookkeeping and valuable items onto the ships. They have already been hidden in the Japanese consulate and transported elsewhere. Japanese naval personnel from the Japanese warships often land in plain clothes. The American warship No. 20 and the French warship "Cairon" arrived in Shantou on the 12th. It is rumored that Japan will dispatch its Magong port fleet to Fuzhou, Xiamen, Shantou, and Guangzhou, so warships from various countries cannot ignore this either. (October 13)

In the Anti-Japanese Climax, Han Fuqu Orders All Sectors to Remain Calm

Jinan Correspondence: Provincial Chairman Han Fuqu, since the occurrence of the Northeast Incident, has repeatedly received orders from the Central Party Headquarters and the National Government to maintain calmness in external affairs and await the central government's resolution. Moreover, Shandong has a large number of Japanese residents, making the situation unique and requiring particularly cautious action to avoid disputes. Yesterday, he specially issued a public notice to all sectors that, from now on, all meetings convened and slogans posted must be subject to review and approval by the Provincial Party Headquarters and the Provincial Government before they can be held. The text of the public notice is recorded below: "Since the beginning of the Northeast Incident, the Central Party Headquarters and the National Government have repeatedly issued orders by telegram, instructing us to maintain calmness and await the central government's legal resolution, which should be followed accordingly. In this critical autumn of survival and extinction, I, as the chairman governing both military and civilian affairs, bear the responsibility of defending the territory and protecting the people. Learning from the past, I have long held the determination to love the country and the people, aiming to turn danger into safety and achieve a final peaceful victory. This humble intention of mine should be shared by all the elders and brothers in Shandong. As for saving the country and seeking survival, it is a sentiment shared by everyone. However, while patriotism is accompanied by enthusiasm, handling affairs requires consideration of the overall situation. If only useless propaganda is carried out, it will only create disputes and may affect local security. My duty is to maintain peace and order and protect the lives and property of the majority of the people in Shandong. I am determined not to allow the misconduct of a few people to lead to unexpected risks. If there is any unrest in the area, it means that I have not fulfilled my duties. Therefore, I am taking precautions to prevent problems and repeatedly admonishing everyone. For this reason, I hereby issue this notice to all sectors of the public, informing you that from now on, I hope everyone will remain calm. If there are any matters such as convening meetings or posting slogans, they must be reviewed and approved by the Provincial Party Headquarters and the Provincial Government in advance before they can be held, so as to be cautious. Indeed, it is appropriate to eliminate troubles before they arise, and it is valuable to think about difficulties when angry. If, in case of carelessness, villains take advantage of the situation to create disturbances under the guise of patriotism, leading to harming the country in the name of loving it and harming the people in the name of caring for them, even if there is regret afterward, it will be too late. All my elders and brothers must think about potential problems and take precautions to ensure peace, jointly maintaining the difficult times. This is my only hope." (19th)

The 44th Meeting of the Executive Yuan

The Executive Yuan held its 44th State Council meeting on the 20th. The attendees were Song Ziwen, Wang Boqun, Yang Shuzhuang, Kong Xiangxi, Lian Shengkai, Liu Ruiheng, and Li Shuhua. Wang Zhijue, Cao Haosen, Zhang Wohua, Lu Bi, and Xu Jingzhi were present as observers. Song Ziwen chaired the meeting. The matters discussed were as follows: (1) Premier Chiang's proposal: To investigate the implementation plans formulated by the former Ministry of Health for various health administration undertakings, it is now proposed to prepare for the establishment of a Central Health Facility Experiment Office. During the preparation period, Health Department Director Liu Ruiheng will be responsible for the preparations. The corresponding proposal is submitted for public decision. Resolution: Approved. (2) Report from the Ministry of Interior: This year's floods have been severe, and emergency relief can only alleviate the immediate situation. The fundamental solution still lies in developing water conservancy. The central government should issue recovery bonds and allocate them according to their importance and urgency, with overall planning. Hubei, Hunan, Jiangsu, Anhui, and other provinces that have been particularly affected by the disaster should be allocated as much as possible. However, relying solely on central recovery bonds is insufficient. Local governments should also find ways to contribute. It is proposed to order the Flood Relief Committee to determine the number of labor and relief workers to be distributed to each province based on the already issued recovery bonds. If there is a shortfall, local governments should be responsible for making up the difference. All projects should be ordered to submit plans based on the approved funds for review and approval and start construction immediately. Are these arrangements appropriate? Requesting instructions. Resolution: Referred to the Flood Relief Committee. (3) Report from the Ministry of Interior: According to the Health Department's report on the revised articles of association of the Central Hospital and the Central Hospital Committee, please review and submit them for record-keeping. After reviewing the revised articles of association, they are generally appropriate and should be approved for record-keeping. A report is submitted for review and implementation. Resolution: Approved for record-keeping.

Local Correspondence: Jinshan

Amid Winter Defense, Banditry is Resurgent. After the capture and execution of major bandits like Taibao, Ashu, Zhu, Amei, etc., local figures fear that the remnants cannot be completely eliminated. Therefore, they continue to bear a substantial amount of expenses for public security. In addition to a stationed provincial security team of one battalion, there are also police teams, water patrol teams, aquatic provincial public security teams, and local defense corps in each district. It can be said that the defense of the small Jinshan area is quite thorough. Unexpectedly, as the autumn harvest of farmers approaches and rents for each granary are about to begin, cases of robbery have occurred one after another, which is unfortunate for the local area. The following is a record: The day before yesterday (the 17th) night, the home of a certain surname in Xiongshan and the home of Chen Jinchang in Fangxiang Township, just half a li away from Zhang, were both robbed clean by bandits, and the victims were injured. Quite Yesterday (the 18th) at midnight, in the Liujia Yanqiao area, the birthplace of bandits, more than 20 bandits suddenly arrived, openly carrying weapons and surrounding the entire town, searching every household without exception. It is said that the Huang surname butcher shop and a certain southern goods store suffered the greatest losses. Although the area is not far from the military and police station, there is no telephone available, so the bandits were able to calmly leave.

Songjiang

Minutes of the Party and Government Talk. The county's party and government agencies held their 31st Party and Government Talk yesterday. County Magistrate Shen presided, and each agency reported on the work status of the past week in order. Subsequently, the County Executive Committee proposed that the rent collection meeting should be convened by the county government, and representatives from the district farmers' association should be added. As a result of the talks, it was passed that the county government should formulate measures and submit them to the next Party and Government Talk for discussion before submitting them to the Department of Civil Affairs for record-keeping. Another item proposed by the County Executive Committee was that, as winter defense is approaching, the county government should be requested to prepare for the establishment of a county defense corps as soon as possible to strengthen defense. As a result of the talks, the county government ordered each district to handle the matter quickly in accordance with the regulations.

Robbery Case in Shiqi Tu. Lu, of Shiqi Tu in the 15th District, was suddenly attacked by seven or eight bandits speaking local dialects while he was sleeping on the night of the 18th. Each held short knives, candles, ropes, etc., and broke into the house, confining the victim in a room. They searched and robbed at will, taking away 80 yuan in paper money and 46 yuan in silver dollars. They then left swaggering. It is learned that a suspect, Shen Bulin, was recently arrested in Ruanxiang Town. It was found that Shen was a fugitive from the previous year's robbery in the tea house. He has now been transferred to the County Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Suzhou

Anti-Japanese Association Seizes a Large Batch of Japanese Goods. After the establishment of the Wu County Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, it detained Japanese goods at the railway station, which were then released without authorization by committee member Gu Baiyu and others. All sectors believe that the procedures were incorrect and expressed dissatisfaction. The County Party Headquarters has resolved to convene a meeting of representatives from all sectors on the 22nd to reorganize the association. Students from the Jian Ding and An Cheng schools, who are part of the inspection team, have seized a large batch of Japanese goods in Che Lun and other ports in recent days. There are ten boxes of oiled paper, five pieces of lead skin, sixty-six boxes of paper goods, ten boxes of yarn, as well as scattered items such as cigarettes and buttons, all of which have been sealed up awaiting identification. The association has telegraphed the Shanghai Anti-Japanese Association, requesting them to send personnel to Suzhou to identify whether the paper goods seized are Japanese goods.

Interception of a Large Number of Hostages in Mochen Town. In the case of the robbery and abduction of 26 hostages in Mochen Town, Changshu, the third district of the local water public security intercepted five hostages, Fan Shaomei, Jiang Yangsheng, Fan Lifu, Zhu Yishi, Fang Songhuai, etc., in Zhouzhuang Township. They were sent to Suzhou yesterday for disposal. Furthermore, the Weiting Township Public Security Sub-bureau discovered hostages Wan Zhangshi, Wan Chaobao, and boatmen Yan Jinbao, Gu Jinbiao, and Guo Rushan. Except for the two boatmen who were sent to the Public Security Bureau for investigation, the two hostages were sent to Guangci Hospital for treatment due to illness.

Wuxi

Anti-Japanese Association Continues to Seize a Large Batch of Enemy Goods. The inspection department of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association in this county has seized many enemy goods in various stores in recent days and handed them over to the identification committee for identification and disposal. The day before yesterday evening, inspectors from the inspection department seized dozens of pieces of privately hidden enemy goods cloth in the private residence of the manager of Xiecheng Yong, located at No. 20 Donghe Tou Lane in the city. They immediately sealed them up for identification and disposal. Upon hearing the news, the merchants of the store rushed to stop them, not allowing them to be taken away. The atmosphere was extremely tense for a while, and the two sides almost clashed. Later, Ji Pu, a standing committee member of the Anti-Japanese Association, came forward to persuade them, and only then did they avoid any excessive actions. After the incident at Xiecheng Yong, the silk, cloth, southern goods, foreign goods, paper, porcelain, electrical materials, hardware, mountain goods, books, western medicine, pigments and other eleven industries convened several meetings. As a result, dozens of representatives were elected to submit a petition to the County Party Headquarters and the County Government, requesting a solution. That night, Chen Chang invited the members of the Party Headquarters to discuss solutions at the County Government in order to find a solution.

Two Ships in Jiangyin Simultaneously Robbed. You Weibiong, the owner of the Jiangyin night ferry, which travels between this county and Jiangyin, set sail from Cheng yesterday afternoon (the 20th) at 8 o'clock, fully loaded with passengers, and arrived in Xishi yesterday morning at 3:30. Suddenly, while passing through the Gaotangwu area of Baitangwu in this county, a covered boat came, and seven bandits jumped out. One bandit, dressed in yellow and carrying four Mauser pistols, ordered the ship to stop. The bandits boarded the ship one after another, turning the cabins upside down and robbing each of the more than 40 passengers. After an hour, they finally took their loot, jumped back into their original boat, and sped away. Upon inspection afterward, it was found that 500 yuan in silver notes entrusted to the Jiangyin Buxiemao Mibu Store to Wuxi Baokang Run were robbed, along with 25 yuan in silver and 5 yuan in corner notes, and 200 corners in small silver dollars from the ship owner, 50 yuan in paper money from passenger Sun Peiji, and 40 yuan in silver dollars entrusted by the Jiangyin Asian Pharmacy. The total loss was more than 700 yuan. The ship owner, You Weibiong, reported to the 5th District Office of the area and forwarded it to the County Government, requesting the arrest of the thieves and the recovery of the stolen goods. At the same time, he sailed the ship to the city and moored it on the river bank under the North Suspension Bridge, reporting to the relevant stores. At the same time, a ship from Jiangyin Nanzha to Xiyi was also stopped by the bandit ship while passing through Dawan in Baitangwu. The bandits boarded the ship and robbed it. The ship owner, Xu Ronglin, was stabbed in both legs by the bandits, and passenger Xu Jingen was also beaten and injured. As a result, cash, jewelry, clothes, and other items were robbed, with a total loss of 788 yuan. The next day, the ship owner, Xu Ronglin, reported the situation to the County Public Security Bureau, requesting the arrest of the thieves.

Jiangyin

The Anti-Japanese Association Was Reorganized for the Second Time, and a Student Union Was Established. On the 10th and 11th of this month (Double Ten Festival), 1,369 bales of Japanese yarn were found in Huacheng, which were then stored in the Anti-Japanese Association. However, Huacheng secretly took away 200 bales. Huacheng insisted that the yarn purchased was from August 21st to September 25th, and that they had paid the national salvation fund and obtained 452 permits and 112 pieces of yarn. Later, the County Party Headquarters and the County Government sent personnel to investigate and await a letter from the Shanghai Anti-Japanese Association to verify the matter. Unexpectedly, it was rumored in society the day before yesterday that Huacheng had spent 4,000 yuan to bribe and redeem the goods. During the enlarged grain remembrance week on the 19th, County Magistrate Peng strongly denied the rumors, saying that if there was any bribery, please report it as much as possible. Subsequently, District Executive Committee member Wang Bingchu gave a speech, saying that this matter was not without cause and should be thoroughly investigated. Furthermore, the Anti-Japanese Association was reorganized yesterday, electing Xi Hanyin and eight others as members, and the oath will be taken on the first of next month.

Changzhou

There Is Already a Way to Seal Up the Goods. The Wu County Chamber of Commerce convened a meeting of various industries on the 20th to discuss the decisions of some merchants to destroy the County Party Headquarters and seal up Japanese goods. As a result, it was resolved that: (1) representatives would be publicly elected to go to the County Party Headquarters, Zhongshan Daily, and Anti-Japanese Association to apologize, and to visit and console the injured staff in the hospital; (2) all items destroyed would be compensated and repaired by the chamber of commerce, and medical expenses would be borne; (3) the arrest and punishment of the culprits would be handled by the government, and if the chamber of commerce had the ability to assist, it would do its best; (4) for the sealing of Japanese goods, in addition to those that have been automatically sealed, they should be automatically sealed by the 22nd of this month, and the industry associations of each industry should affix seals for the Anti-Japanese Association to inspect.

Zhenjiang

Results of the Re-election of the Business Corps. The Zhenjiang Business Corps held a re-election meeting yesterday. More than 20 people, including Yang Guangyu and Zhou Zigen, attended. As a result of the election, more than 30 people, including Yang Guangyu, Zhou Zigen, and Xie Yansheng, were elected as directors, and Yang Guangyu, Xie Yansheng, Zhu Jiheng, Zhang Yunshao, and Hu Jianchun were mutually elected as standing directors. Yang Guangyu was also mutually elected as chairman of the board, Lu Xiaobo was elected as corps leader, and Guo Daomi was elected as deputy corps leader. After the election, the meeting adjourned, but corps leader Lu Xiaobo sent a letter to the association that evening, firmly resigning and recommending Guo Daomi to fill the vacancy. Recent News on the Embezzlement Case in the Highway Bureau. Sun Shiqin, the chief engineer of the Highway Bureau of the Department of Construction, Feng Qi, the chief accountant, and engineers Lu Fangcai and Qin Lao Chong, etc., forged and reimbursed expenses and privately engraved more than 180 seals of major stores along the road in a hotel in the city. After the case was discovered, they were sent to the court. After the court opened an investigation, it detained Sun Baoqin and seven others, and released Yu Qi and four others on bail. The Department of Construction has sent personnel to the court to investigate the accounts to clarify the truth and facilitate the filing of a public prosecution. Furthermore, it is learned that the court prosecutor interrogated the detained Sun Qin, Feng Qi, Qin Zhichong, Lu Fangcai, Sun Gongfu, and other in court again yesterday morning for a long time. As a result, Sun Gongfu was ordered to post bail and wait for trial. It is said that the procedures for this case are numerous and cannot be concluded in a short time.

Nantong

Zhang Ji's Wanted Order Cancelled. The Provincial Government, upon the order of the Executive Yuan, issued a notice to the Higher Court, the Shanghai and Nanjing Municipal Governments, and the counties and bureaus of the Department of Civil Affairs, canceling Zhang Ji's wanted order. The matter of returning property will be handled separately.

Relief for Local Financial Difficulties. Nantong's local finances have fallen into a desperate situation. Currently, debts are being used to maintain the status quo. After discussion at the county's administrative meeting, the local budget for the 20th year, all non-urgent agencies, were suspended or allocated separately in accordance with the law. As for those that can be reduced, they were reduced accordingly. In addition, the Finance Bureau established a busy canal and old debt cleanup committee to recover unpaid taxes. At the same time, it presented a plan to the province to increase the tax on stove land by two yuan and jointly present to the Provincial Government, requesting that the stove land be assigned to the province and the tax be increased.

Yangzhou

Execution of the Gang Leader of the Bandit Squad. Wang Chuanren, the squad leader of the Yixing County Police Team, colluded with the bandits Wang Wenbiao, etc., and only shot and killed Che Qihong's mother, Che Jiangshi, in Chejiadang. After Hu Ziqing, Xu Ziying, Zhang Renjie, etc., reported the matter to the Superintendent Zhang for Suppression, who ordered Zhang Yineng, the fourth regiment leader of the Security Team stationed in Yi, to investigate and confirm the facts, he ordered the county to send him to Yang for legal action. Now, after the Superintendent's Office investigated the matter, it was confirmed that Wang Wenbiao and the fugitive bandits Wang Changyi and Li Xinggao discussed the matter in advance at Wangjiaji, and Wang Chuanren allowed the fugitive bandit Wang Changyi to carry a gun and live in his home without denial. Therefore, in accordance with the regulations for punishing bandits, he was sentenced to death and executed by shooting on the afternoon of the 20th. Immediately afterward, the charges were announced as a warning.

Xinghua

Education Representatives Go to Beijing to Appeal. Xinghua is located in a low-lying area, and this year's flood has been severe. All industries have been hit hard, especially education, which has no way out. Teachers are feeling the hardship of life and have repeatedly presented the matter to the authorities for relief. The hall committee recently visited Xing, but they also felt helpless. In a state of panic, they recommended the acting director of the Education Bureau, Gao Yangchun, and the executive secretary of the County Education Association, Pan Dejun, to go to the province and Beijing to appeal. It is said that they have crossed the river and have been busy running around the government offices for days.

Hangzhou

Guangchang Bandit Gang Is on the Verge of Invading Zhejiang Again. After the Changxing Coal Mine Bureau was robbed, the director of the bureau was shot and killed, and all the firearms were confiscated. Afterward, the security team chased them and recovered a machine gun and many wooden shell rifles, killing more than ten bandits. The rest scattered and fled. Zhu Mingtao, the director of the Provincial Security Department, received a telegram from the pursuing troops, stating that the gang of bandits, Zheng Erfenzi and others, numbering three or four hundred, had been severely attacked by two companies led by Zeng and were mostly hiding in the areas bordering Guangchang. They were also attacked from the rear by Xu Tuan and Wang Ying of Anhui Province, leaving them with no way to escape. They are on the verge of making a comeback. After receiving the report, the Provincial Government urgently telegraphed Wang Zhiqi, the commander of the 2nd Regiment stationed in Hu, yesterday (the 21st), ordering him to personally lead his troops to the area to command the two companies led by Dong and Zeng to advance and suppress the bandits. As for the one battalion of the Jiangsu Provincial Security Team led by Vice-Chairman Zeng, it arrived in Si'an the night before last and will discuss joint suppression measures with the Zhejiang Security Team today. Furthermore, it is learned that Zeng Commander has sent a special telegram yesterday reporting the details of the situation.

Anti-Japanese Association Seized Japanese Goods Again Yesterday. Chen Yuanzheng and Wang Jinzhang, inspectors of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association in Hangzhou, inspected Japanese goods at the city station yesterday and seized ten pieces of Dafengchang Xiechang vinegar, five pieces of Hongyu Clothing Store's silk, and one piece of Taihe Clothing Store's serge, along with Dafeng's harmonica buttons and other items in Shen Da Transfer Company and the post office. All were detained and sealed for disposal.

Taizhou

Organizing a Volunteer Corps. Since hearing the news from the eastern provinces, the merchants of silk, cloth, and Guang goods in Haimen, Linhai, have been extremely indignant. They discussed the matter together and decided to organize a volunteer corps. The members of the corps will be filled by merchants of the two industries. The public associations of the two industries have been selected as the corps headquarters. Regulations have been formulated, and the local Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association has been requested to send a military training officer to provide daily training. It will be implemented soon.

Letters Received

Letter from the Xiaoshan County Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association

To the esteemed editor: After reading a news item in your newspaper on the 18th of this month, "Xiaoshan Flood Relief Association Borrowing the Association's Premises Caused Disputes," this Association has learned that the Nanhuo Industry Association of our county deliberately engaged in reactionary sabotage of the national salvation movement. On the 14th of this month, they gathered thugs, broke into this Association, shouting slogans such as "Down with the Party Headquarters!" and "Down with the Anti-Japanese Association!" They forcibly sealed the main entrance of this Association and left with whistles and shouts. This Association has sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau requesting that the main culprit, Wang Zancheng, be arrested, which has been done. Therefore, we are sending this letter to clarify the truth, hoping that you will publish it in the "Letters Received" section. Xiaoshan County Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association General Affairs Department.

To be held concurrently with Memorial Week.

Su Education Department, Director's Notice: JiangSu Education Bureaus, all levels of schools, recently approved the Chinese Kuomintang Jiangsu Provincial Executive Committee letter, please forward to all county education bureaus with the county party department to notify all schools, in the morning of the 26th of this month, to hold a Memorial Week and hold a Memorial Assembly for the National Crisis simultaneously, at that time, all lower the flag, mourn for three minutes, and invite personnel familiar with Chinese and Japanese history and geography or party staff to give speeches on the history of national humiliation and the Japanese people's forceful occupation of the three northeastern provinces. In addition to sending telegrams, please comply with the above instructions, etc. 本埠 (Local Port)

United Association of Anti-Japanese National Salvation Societies of Various Universities

丨Seventeenth Executive Committee Meeting丨
